## ๐ Authentication

### Supabase Client

**Location:** `src/api/supabaseClient.js`

```javascript
import { supabase } from '@/api/supabaseClient';

// Sign Up
const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
  email: 'user@example.com',
  password: 'secure-password'
});

// Sign In
const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
  email: 'user@example.com',
  password: 'secure-password'
});

// Sign Out
const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();

// Get Current User
const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
```

### AuthContext

**Location:** `src/contexts/AuthContext.jsx`

```javascript
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

function MyComponent() {
  const { user, signIn, signOut, loading } = useAuth();
  
  if (loading) return <div>Loading...</div>;
  
  return (
    <div>
      {user ? (
        <button onClick={signOut}>Sign Out</button>
      ) : (
        <button onClick={() => signIn(email, password)}>Sign In</button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Methods:**
- `signIn(email, password)` - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฏุฎูู
- `signUp(email, password)` - ุฅูุดุงุก ุญุณุงุจ
- `signOut()` - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฎุฑูุฌ
- `user` - ุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ุงูุญุงูู
- `loading` - ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุชุญููู

### 1. Text Analyzer Enhanced

**Location:** `src/Components/upload/TextAnalyzerEnhanced.js`

#### analyzeAndCleanText()

ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุดุงููุฉ ูููุตูุต ูุน ุชูููู 60-70% ูู ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู LLM.

```javascript

  text,              // ุงููุต ุงูุฃุตูู
  language,          // 'ar' | 'en'
  callbacks          // Object with start, progress, complete
);
```

**Parameters:**

| Name | Type | Required | Description |
|------|------|----------|-------------|
| text | string | โ | ุงููุต ุงููุฑุงุฏ ูุนุงูุฌุชู |
| language | string | โ | ูุบุฉ ุงููุต ('ar' or 'en') |
| callbacks | object | โ | ุฏูุงู callback ููุชูุฏู |

**Callbacks Structure:**

```javascript
{
  start: (stageName) => void,      // ุนูุฏ ุจุฏุก ูุฑุญูุฉ
  progress: (stageName, data) => void,  // ุฃุซูุงุก ุงูุชูุฏู
  complete: (stageName) => void     // ุนูุฏ ุงูุชูุงู ูุฑุญูุฉ
}
```

**Return Value:**

```javascript
{
  cleaned_text: string,           // ุงููุต ุงูููุธู
  statistics: {
    original_words: number,       // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช ุงูุฃุตูู
    final_words: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช ุงูููุงุฆู
    original_chars: number,       // ุนุฏุฏ ุงูุฃุญุฑู ุงูุฃุตูู
    final_chars: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงูุฃุญุฑู ุงูููุงุฆู
    removed_pages: number,        // ุงูุตูุญุงุช ุงููุญุฐููุฉ
    removed_toc: boolean,         // ูู ุชู ุญุฐู ุงูููุฑุณุ
    removed_duplicates: number,   // ุงูุชูุฑุงุฑุงุช ุงููุญุฐููุฉ
    chapters_detected: number,    // ุงููุตูู ุงูููุชุดูุฉ
    processing_time: number       // ููุช ุงููุนุงูุฌุฉ (ms)
  },
  chapters: [
    {
      title: string,              // ุนููุงู ุงููุตู
      content: string,            // ูุญุชูู ุงููุตู
      wordCount: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช
      number: number              // ุฑูู ุงููุตู
    }

    score: number,                // 0-100
    issues: string[],             // ุงููุดุงูู ุงูููุชุดูุฉ
    suggestions: string[]         // ุงูุชุฑุงุญุงุช ุงูุชุญุณูู

```

**Example:**

```javascript

  start: (stage) => console.log(`๐ ุจุฏุฃ: ${stage}`),
  progress: (stage, data) => {
    console.log(`โณ ${stage}: ${data.progress}%`);

  complete: (stage) => console.log(`โ ุงูุชูู: ${stage}`)
```

#### duplicateDetector

**Location:** `src/utils/nlp/duplicateDetector.js`

```javascript

// ูุดู ุงูุชูุฑุงุฑุงุช

  threshold: 0.8,        // 80% ุชุดุงุจู
  minLength: 50          // ุงูุญุฏ ุงูุฃุฏูู ููุทูู
});

// ุฅุฒุงูุฉ ุงูุชูุฑุงุฑุงุช
```

**Options:**

```javascript
{
  threshold: number,      // 0-1 (default: 0.8)
  minLength: number,      // minimum chars (default: 50)
  method: 'shingling' | 'lcs'  // algorithm (default: 'shingling')
}
```

### 3. ChunkProcessor

**Location:** `src/utils/ChunkProcessor.js`

ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูุตูุต ูุจูุฑุฉ (ุญุชู 200k ูููุฉ) ุจุทุฑููุฉ ูุชูุงุฒูุฉ.

```javascript

  chunkSize: 10000,        // ูููุงุช ููู chunk
  overlap: 500,            // overlap ุจูู chunks
  maxConcurrent: 3         // ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูุชูุงุฒูุฉ
});

  largeText,
  async (chunk) => {
    // ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูู chunk
    return await analyzeChunk(chunk);
  },
  (progress) => {

```

**Methods:**

| Method | Parameters | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|

### 4. CacheManager

**Location:** `src/lib/cache/CacheManager.js`

ูุธุงู ุชุฎุฒูู ูุคูุช ุซูุงุฆู (Memory + IndexedDB).

```javascript

const cache = new CacheManager({
  namespace: 'nlp',
  ttl: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000  // 24 hours
});

// Set
await cache.set('key', data);

// Get
const data = await cache.get('key');

// Delete
await cache.delete('key');

// Clear all
await cache.clear();
```

**Features:**
- โ Memory cache (ุณุฑูุน)
- โ IndexedDB cache (ุฏุงุฆู)
- โ TTL support
- โ Auto-cleanup
- โ Compression

```javascript
  fontFamily: 'Arial'
});

  metadata: {
    author: 'ุงููุคูู',

```

### PDFGenerator

**Location:** `src/utils/export/PDFGenerator.js`

```javascript
import PDFGenerator from '@/utils/export/PDFGenerator';

const generator = new PDFGenerator();

const blob = await generator.generate(manuscript, {
  includeTableOfContents: true,
  rtl: true,
  fontSize: 12,
  fontFamily: 'Arial',
  pageSize: 'A4',
  margins: { top: 20, bottom: 20, left: 20, right: 20 }
});

// Download
const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
const a = document.createElement('a');
a.href = url;
a.download = 'book.pdf';
a.click();
```

## โ๏ธ Error Handling

### Error Types

```javascript
// NLP Errors
class NLPError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'NLPError';
    this.code = code;
  }
}

// Export Errors
class ExportError extends Error {
  constructor(message, format) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'ExportError';
    this.format = format;
  }
}

// API Errors
class APIError extends Error {
  constructor(message, status) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'APIError';
    this.status = status;
  }
}
```

---

### Error Handling Best Practices

```javascript
try {
  const result = await analyzeAndCleanText(text, 'ar', callbacks);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof NLPError) {
    console.error('NLP Error:', error.code, error.message);
    // Handle NLP-specific error
  } else if (error instanceof ExportError) {
    console.error('Export Error:', error.format, error.message);
    // Handle export-specific error
  } else {
    console.error('Unknown Error:', error);
    // Handle unknown error
  }
}
```

---

### ErrorBoundary Component

```javascript
import ErrorBoundary from '@/Components/ErrorBoundary';

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <YourComponent />
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}
```

```javascript
    showToast('ูุนูููุฉ', 'info');
```

[products/shadow-seven-publisher/LEGAL_SENTINEL_PROMPT.md]
================================================================================

---
title: Legal Sentinel Prompt v1.0
owner: MRF Sovereign Agency
scope: Publishing compliance screening for manuscripts by territory
---

# Legal Sentinel (SENT_03)

## Role
Act as the compliance officer for the Industrial Publishing Agency. Your task is to screen manuscript content by target territory and return a structured compliance report with explicit pass/fail gates and required edits. You do not provide legal advice; you flag risks and enforce internal publishing policy.

## Core Objectives
- Enforce territory-specific publishing constraints.
- Detect legal, regulatory, and reputational risks.
- Produce a clear decision: PASS, PASS_WITH_EDITS, or FAIL.
- Provide exact sections or examples that triggered a flag.

## Inputs
- `territory`: primary publishing country.
- `manuscript`: raw text (may be split into blocks).
- `metadata`: author name, genre, target audience, marketing claims.

## Output Format (strict JSON)
{
  "territory": "<string>",
  "decision": "PASS | PASS_WITH_EDITS | FAIL",
  "severity_summary": {
    "critical": <int>,
    "high": <int>,
    "medium": <int>,
    "low": <int>
  },
  "flags": [
    {
      "severity": "CRITICAL | HIGH | MEDIUM | LOW",
      "category": "defamation | hate_speech | privacy | IP | public_order | religious_sensitivity | political_content | adult_content | medical_claims | financial_claims | cybersecurity | data_protection | minors",
      "excerpt": "<short excerpt>",
      "location": "<chapter/section/page if available>",
      "reason": "<why it violates or risks policy>",
      "required_action": "REMOVE | REWRITE | REDACT | FACT_CHECK | LEGAL_REVIEW",
      "territory_basis": "<territory-specific rule>"
    }
  ],
  "required_edits": [
    "<short actionable edit instructions>"
  ],
  "notes": [
    "<non-blocking advisory notes>"
  ]
}

## Global Baseline Rules (apply to all territories)
- No defamation of identifiable individuals or organizations without verifiable sources.
- No hate speech or incitement against protected groups.
- No disclosure of private personal data (addresses, phone numbers, IDs) without consent.
- No plagiarism or unlicensed IP use.
- No explicit sexual content involving minors; any such content is an immediate FAIL.
- No instructions that materially enable violence, self-harm, or cybercrime.
- Marketing and medical claims must be clearly labeled as opinion or supported by citations.

## Territory Matrix (enforced on top of global rules)

### United States (US)
- Defamation risk is high when accusations are not clearly marked as opinion or lack sourcing.
- Right of publicity: do not use a living personโs name or likeness commercially without consent.
- Copyright: avoid substantial similarity and unlicensed derivative works.
- Medical and financial advice must include disclaimers and avoid guaranteed outcomes.

### European Union (EU/EEA)
- GDPR: remove or anonymize personal data unless explicit consent exists.
- Strong privacy protections; avoid identifying private individuals.
- Hate speech and extremist content are strictly disallowed.
- Health and financial claims require evidence and non-misleading language.

### United Kingdom (UK)
- Defamation law favors claimants; avoid unverifiable allegations.
- Passing off and trademark confusion risks are elevated.
- Extremism content is prohibited; terrorism glorification is a FAIL.

### Kingdom of Saudi Arabia (KSA)
- Strong restrictions on blasphemy and religious disparagement.
- Political content criticizing leadership or state institutions is high risk.
- Adult content is heavily restricted; explicit sexual content is a FAIL.
- Respect cultural norms around modesty and public order.

### United Arab Emirates (UAE)
- High sensitivity to public order and morality violations.
- Religious insults, defamation of leaders, and pornography are prohibited.
- Content that could be interpreted as incitement or destabilization is disallowed.

### Egypt
- Restrictions on insulting religion, public morals, and state institutions.
- Content that could be construed as defamation of officials is high risk.
- Adult content and explicit sexual description are prohibited.

## Decision Rules
- Any CRITICAL flag triggers FAIL.
- Two or more HIGH flags trigger FAIL unless all are remediable with targeted edits.
- MEDIUM flags require PASS_WITH_EDITS.
- LOW flags may still be listed as advisory notes.

## Agent Behavior
- Be precise: cite excerpts and locations.
- Be conservative: when uncertain, escalate to LEGAL_REVIEW.
- Do not generate legal interpretations; enforce internal publishing policy only.

ุจุนุฏูุง ุฃูุดุฆ Bucket ุจุงุณู `manuscripts` ูู Storage (ุงุฌุนู ุงููุฑุงุกุฉ ุนุงูุฉ ููุชุทููุฑ ููุทุ ูุดุฏูุฏูุง ููุฅูุชุงุฌ).

### 2. ุฅูุดุงุก Database Schema
```sql
-- manuscripts table
CREATE TABLE manuscripts (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  title TEXT NOT NULL,
  author TEXT,
  content TEXT,
  chapters JSONB,
  word_count INTEGER,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft',
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- compliance_rules table
CREATE TABLE compliance_rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  rule_type TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- cover_designs table
CREATE TABLE cover_designs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  manuscript_id UUID REFERENCES manuscripts(id),
  image_url TEXT,
  prompt TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- processing_jobs table
CREATE TABLE processing_jobs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  manuscript_id UUID REFERENCES manuscripts(id),
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
  progress INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);
```

### 3. ุฅูุดุงุก Storage Bucket

# Project Audit Skill - AI Execution Guide\n\n## Purpose\n\nThis guide enables any AI agent to execute the project audit skill with 100% accuracy, regardless of project type, complexity, or state.\n\n---\n\n## Core Logic Flow\n\n```\nINPUT: Project (ZIP/Folder/Repo)\n  โ\n[Phase 1] Reception & Analysis\n  โโ Extract project\n  โโ Identify type\n  โโ Document state\n  โโ Create backup\n  โ\n[Phase 2] Deep Code Analysis\n  โโ Read critical files\n  โโ Analyze architecture\n  โโ Map components\n  โโ Document flows\n  โ\n[Phase 3] Component Inventory\n  โโ Frontend components\n  โโ Backend services\n  โโ Utilities\n  โโ Integrations\n  โ\n[Phase 4] Testing & Validation\n  โโ Install dependencies\n  โโ Run build\n  โโ Execute tests\n  โโ Check errors\n  โ\n[Phase 5] Gap Analysis\n  โโ Compare vs requirements\n  โโ List missing\n  โโ Assess completion %\n  โโ Prioritize gaps\n  โ\n[Phase 6] Gap Filling\n  โโ Database schema\n  โโ Authentication\n  โโ API endpoints\n  โโ Export functions\n  โโ AI/ML features\n  โโ Deployment\n  โ\n[Phase 7] Code Writing\n  โโ Follow conventions\n  โโ Add error handling\n  โโ Add validation\n  โโ Write docs\n  โโ Create tests\n  โ\n[Phase 8] Quality Assurance\n  โโ Code review\n  โโ Run tests\n  โโ Check quality\n  โโ Verify docs\n  โโ Security audit\n  โ\n[Phase 9] Final Packaging\n  โโ Create ZIP\n  โโ Create manifest\n  โโ Write docs\n  โโ Create reports\n  โ\n[Phase 10] Final Delivery\n  โโ Verify tests\n  โโ Confirm build\n  โโ Check docs\n  โโ Validate requirements\n  โโ Sign off\n  โ\nOUTPUT: Complete Project ZIP + Reports (100% Confidence)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Phase-by-Phase Execution\n\n### Phase 1: Project Reception & Initial Analysis\n\n**Objective**: Understand project structure and type\n\n**Actions**:\n```bash\n# 1. Extract project\nunzip project.zip -d /working/directory\ncd /working/directory\n\n# 2. List all files\nfind . -type f | head -50\n\n# 3. Check project type\nls -la | grep -E \"package.json|requirements.txt|go.mod|pom.xml|Dockerfile\"\n\n# 4. Count files\nfind . -type f | wc -l\n\n# 5. Get size\ndu -sh .\n```\n\n**Decision Tree**:\n```\nProject Type?\nโโ package.json exists?\nโ  โโ YES โ Node.js/JavaScript project\nโ  โ  โโ tsconfig.json? โ TypeScript\nโ  โ  โโ vite.config.js? โ Vite\nโ  โ  โโ next.config.js? โ Next.js\nโ  โ  โโ expo.config.js? โ React Native/Expo\nโ  โโ NO โ Check next\nโโ requirements.txt exists?\nโ  โโ YES โ Python project\nโ  โ  โโ django? โ Django\nโ  โ  โโ flask? โ Flask\nโ  โ  โโ fastapi? โ FastAPI\nโ  โโ NO โ Check next\nโโ go.mod exists?\nโ  โโ YES โ Go project\nโ  โโ NO โ Check next\nโโ pom.xml exists?\nโ  โโ YES โ Java/Maven project\nโ  โโ NO โ Check next\nโโ Dockerfile exists?\n   โโ YES โ Containerized project\n   โโ NO โ Generic project\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Project type identified\n- File count\n- Directory structure\n- Backup created\n\n---\n\n### Phase 2: Deep Code Analysis\n\n**Objective**: Understand codebase completely\n\n**Critical Files to Read** (in order):\n1. `README.md` - Project overview\n2. `package.json` or equivalent - Dependencies, scripts\n3. `app.config.ts` or `config.js` - Configuration\n4. `.env.example` - Environment variables\n5. `Dockerfile` - Deployment info\n6. Main entry point (`App.jsx`, `index.js`, `main.py`)\n7. API routes/endpoints file\n8. Database schema file (if exists)\n\n**Analysis Steps**:\n```\nFor each critical file:\n1. Read complete content\n2. Extract key information\n3. Identify dependencies\n4. Note configuration\n5. Document structure\n```\n\n**Architecture Analysis**:\n```\nFrontend (if applicable):\nโโ Framework (React, Vue, Angular, etc.)\nโโ State management (Redux, Zustand, Context, etc.)\nโโ Routing (React Router, Next.js, etc.)\nโโ Styling (CSS, Tailwind, Styled Components, etc.)\nโโ Component structure\n\nBackend (if applicable):\nโโ Framework (Express, FastAPI, Django, etc.)\nโโ Database (PostgreSQL, MongoDB, etc.)\nโโ Authentication (JWT, OAuth, Sessions, etc.)\nโโ API structure (REST, GraphQL, etc.)\nโโ Business logic\n\nDatabase (if applicable):\nโโ Type (SQL, NoSQL, etc.)\nโโ Schema (tables, collections)\nโโ Relationships\nโโ Indexes\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Architecture diagram (text-based)\n- Technology stack\n- Dependencies list\n- Configuration overview\n\n---\n\n### Phase 3: Component Inventory\n\n**Objective**: Catalog all existing components\n\n**Frontend Components** (if applicable):\n```bash\n# Find all component files\nfind ./src/components -type f -name \"*.jsx\" -o -name \"*.tsx\" | wc -l\nfind ./src/components -type f -name \"*.jsx\" -o -name \"*.tsx\" | sort\n\n# Count by type\nfind ./src/components -type f -name \"*Button*\"\nfind ./src/components -type f -name \"*Form*\"\nfind ./src/components -type f -name \"*Modal*\"\n```\n\n**Backend Services** (if applicable):\n```bash\n# Find API routes\nfind ./src/routes -type f -name \"*.js\"\nfind ./src/api -type f -name \"*.py\"\n\n# Find models\nfind ./src/models -type f\nfind ./src/database -type f\n```\n\n**Utilities & Helpers**:\n```bash\n# Find utility files\nfind ./src/utils -type f\nfind ./src/lib -type f\nfind ./src/helpers -type f\n```\n\n**Inventory Template**:\n```\nFrontend Components: _____ total\nโโ Custom components: _____\nโโ UI library components: _____\nโโ Pages/Screens: _____\nโโ Hooks: _____\n\nBackend Services: _____ total\nโโ API endpoints: _____\nโโ Database models: _____\nโโ Middleware: _____\nโโ Services: _____\n\nUtilities: _____ total\nโโ Helpers: _____\nโโ Validators: _____\nโโ Formatters: _____\nโโ Constants: _____\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Component count by type\n- Component list with descriptions\n- Dependencies between components\n\n---\n\n### Phase 4: Testing & Validation\n\n**Objective**: Verify everything works\n\n**Build Process**:\n```bash\n# Install dependencies\nnpm install  # or pip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Check for errors\nnpm install 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\\|warn\"\n\n# Run build\nnpm run build 2>&1\n\n# Check build output\nls -lah dist/ 2>/dev/null || ls -lah build/ 2>/dev/null\n```\n\n**Test Execution**:\n```bash\n# Run tests\nnpm run test 2>&1\n\n# Check coverage\nnpm run test:coverage 2>&1\n\n# Parse results\n# Look for: \"passing\", \"failing\", \"coverage\"\n```\n\n**Dependency Check**:\n```bash\n# Audit dependencies\nnpm audit 2>&1\n\n# Check outdated\nnpm outdated 2>&1\n\n# Count packages\nnpm list 2>&1 | grep -c \"โโโ\"\n```\n\n**Validation Checklist**:\n- [ ] Dependencies install successfully\n- [ ] Build completes without errors\n- [ ] Tests run successfully\n- [ ] No critical vulnerabilities\n- [ ] No console errors\n\n**Output**:\n- Build status (โ/โ)\n- Test results (pass/fail count)\n- Dependency audit results\n- Error/warning log\n\n---\n\n### Phase 5: Gap Analysis\n\n**Objective**: Identify what's missing\n\n**Comparison Matrix**:\n```\nComponent          | Expected | Found | Status\nโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ\nDatabase Schema    |    โ    |  โ   | MISSING\nAuthentication UI  |    โ    |  โ   | MISSING\nExport Functions   |    โ    |  โ   | MISSING\nAPI Endpoints      |    โ    |  โ   | COMPLETE\nTesting            |    โ    |  โ๏ธ   | PARTIAL\nDocumentation      |    โ    |  โ๏ธ   | PARTIAL\nDeployment Config  |    โ    |  โ   | MISSING\n```\n\n**Gap Prioritization**:\n```\nCritical (Blocks Core Functionality):\n1. Database Schema\n2. Authentication\n3. Core API Endpoints\n\nHigh (Affects Major Features):\n1. Export Functions\n2. Error Handling\n3. Input Validation\n\nMedium (Nice to Have):\n1. Advanced Features\n2. Optimizations\n3. Polish\n\nLow (Polish):\n1. Comments\n2. Formatting\n3. Minor improvements\n```\n\n**Completion Percentage Calculation**:\n```\nTotal Components: 100\nImplemented: 80\nCompletion: 80/100 = 80%\n\nBy Category:\nโโ Frontend: 85%\nโโ Backend: 75%\nโโ Database: 60%\nโโ Testing: 70%\nโโ Documentation: 50%\nโโ Deployment: 0%\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Gap list (prioritized)\n- Completion percentage\n- Impact analysis\n- Effort estimation\n\n---\n\n### Phase 6: Gap Filling\n\n**Objective**: Implement all missing components\n\n**Gap Filling Strategy**:\n\n#### 1. Database Schema (if missing)\n```sql\n-- Analyze existing database usage\n-- Design schema based on requirements\n-- Create migration files\n-- Add RLS policies (if Supabase)\n-- Create indexes\n```\n\n**Template**:\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n  password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Add RLS\nALTER TABLE users ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\nCREATE POLICY \"Users can view own data\" ON users\n  FOR SELECT USING (auth.uid() = id);\n```\n\n#### 2. Authentication (if missing)\n```jsx\n// Create login page\n// Create signup page\n// Create profile page\n// Implement session management\n// Add password recovery\n```\n\n**Template**:\n```jsx\nexport function AuthPage() {\n  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');\n  const [isLogin, setIsLogin] = useState(true);\n\n  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    // Implement auth logic\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>\n      {/* Form fields */}\n    </form>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n#### 3. API Endpoints (if missing)\n```js\n// Design API structure\n// Implement CRUD operations\n// Add validation\n// Add error handling\n// Write API docs\n```\n\n**Template**:\n```js\napp.post('/api/items', async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    // Validate input\n    const { name, description } = req.body;\n    if (!name) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Name required' });\n\n    // Create item\n    const item = await db.items.create({ name, description });\n\n    // Return response\n    res.json({ success: true, data: item });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });\n  }\n});\n```\n\n#### 4. Export Functions (if missing)\n```js\n// PDF export with RTL support\n// EPUB export\n// DOCX export\n// ZIP packaging\n```\n\n**Template**:\n```js\nexport async function exportToPDF(content, filename) {\n  const doc = new PDFDocument();\n  doc.fontSize(12).text(content);\n  doc.pipe(fs.createWriteStream(filename));\n  doc.end();\n}\n```\n\n#### 5. AI/ML Features (if missing)\n```js\n// Implement AI agents\n// Add processing functions\n// Create validation\n```\n\n#### 6. Deployment (if missing)\n```dockerfile\n# Create Dockerfile\n# Create docker-compose.yml\n# Create deployment scripts\n```\n\n**Template**:\n```dockerfile\nFROM node:20-alpine\nWORKDIR /app\nCOPY package*.json ./\nRUN npm install\nCOPY . .\nRUN npm run build\nEXPOSE 3000\nCMD [\"npm\", \"start\"]\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- All gap implementations\n- Code files created\n- Tests written\n- Documentation updated\n\n---\n\n### Phase 7: Code Writing & Implementation\n\n**Objective**: Write production-quality code\n\n**Code Standards**:\n```javascript\n// 1. Follow project conventions\n// 2. Use consistent naming\n// 3. Add error handling\n// 4. Include input validation\n// 5. Write JSDoc comments\n// 6. Create unit tests\n\n/**\n * Processes user data and returns formatted result\n * @param {Object} user - User object\n * @param {string} user.name - User name\n * @param {string} user.email - User email\n * @returns {Promise<Object>} Formatted user data\n * @throws {Error} If user data is invalid\n */\nasync function processUser(user) {\n  // Validate input\n  if (!user || !user.email) {\n    throw new Error('User email is required');\n  }\n\n  try {\n    // Process data\n    const result = await formatUser(user);\n    return result;\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Error processing user:', error);\n    throw error;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Testing Template**:\n```javascript\ndescribe('processUser', () => {\n  it('should process valid user data', async () => {\n    const user = { name: 'John', email: 'john@example.com' };\n    const result = await processUser(user);\n    expect(result).toBeDefined();\n    expect(result.email).toBe('john@example.com');\n  });\n\n  it('should throw error for missing email', async () => {\n    const user = { name: 'John' };\n    await expect(processUser(user)).rejects.toThrow();\n  });\n});\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Production-ready code\n- Comprehensive tests\n- JSDoc documentation\n- Error handling\n\n---\n\n### Phase 8: Quality Assurance\n\n**Objective**: Ensure everything meets standards\n\n**QA Checklist**:\n```bash\n# 1. Run linter\nnpm run lint 2>&1\n\n# 2. Check formatting\nnpm run format 2>&1\n\n# 3. Type checking\nnpm run type-check 2>&1\n\n# 4. Run tests\nnpm run test 2>&1\n\n# 5. Check coverage\nnpm run test:coverage 2>&1\n\n# 6. Build\nnpm run build 2>&1\n\n# 7. Security audit\nnpm audit 2>&1\n```\n\n**Validation Criteria**:\n- โ No linting errors\n- โ No formatting issues\n- โ No type errors\n- โ All tests passing\n- โ >80% code coverage\n- โ Build successful\n- โ No security vulnerabilities\n- โ Documentation complete\n\n**Output**:\n- QA report\n- Test coverage report\n- Security audit report\n- Build log\n\n---\n\n### Phase 9: Final Packaging\n\n**Objective**: Create deliverable package\n\n**Packaging Steps**:\n```bash\n# 1. Create ZIP\nzip -r project-complete-v1.0.0.zip . \\\n  -x \"*/node_modules/*\" \"*/.git/*\" \"*/dist/*\" \"*/.env*\"\n\n# 2. Verify ZIP\nunzip -l project-complete-v1.0.0.zip | head -30\n\n# 3. Check size\nls -lh project-complete-v1.0.0.zip\n```\n\n**Documentation to Create**:\n1. `PROJECT_COMPLETION_REPORT.md` - Complete project status\n2. `SETUP_GUIDE.md` - Installation and setup\n3. `DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md` - Deployment instructions\n4. `API_DOCUMENTATION.md` - API reference\n5. `TROUBLESHOOTING.md` - Common issues and solutions\n\n**Output**:\n- Complete project ZIP\n- Completion report\n- Setup guide\n- Deployment guide\n- API documentation\n\n---\n\n### Phase 10: Final Delivery\n\n**Objective**: Deliver with 100% confidence\n\n**Final Verification Checklist**:\n```\nโ All tests passing (100%)\nโ Build successful\nโ No console errors\nโ No security vulnerabilities\nโ Documentation complete\nโ Code coverage >80%\nโ Performance acceptable\nโ Accessibility compliant\nโ All requirements met\nโ Ready for production\n```\n\n**Confidence Metrics**:\n```\nCode Quality:     โ 95%\nTest Coverage:    โ 85%\nDocumentation:    โ 100%\nSecurity:         โ 100%\nPerformance:      โ 90%\nAccessibility:    โ 85%\nCompletion:       โ 100%\n\nOVERALL CONFIDENCE: โ 100%\n```\n\n**Output**:\n- Complete project ZIP\n- All documentation\n- Completion report\n- Sign-off confirmation\n\n---\n\n## AI Decision Making\n\n### When to Skip Steps\n\n**Skip Phase 4 (Testing) if**:\n- Project has no tests\n- Build fails with missing dependencies\n- โ Action: Document and continue to Phase 5\n\n**Skip Phase 6 (Gap Filling) if**:\n- Project is already 100% complete\n- โ Action: Skip to Phase 8 (QA)\n\n**Skip Phase 7 (Code Writing) if**:\n- No gaps to fill\n- โ Action: Skip to Phase 8 (QA)\n\n### When to Iterate\n\n**Iterate if**:\n- Tests fail after changes\n- Build fails\n- Security issues found\n- โ Action: Fix and re-run QA\n\n### Error Handling\n\n**If build fails**:\n1. Check error message\n2. Identify root cause\n3. Fix issue\n4. Re-run build\n5. Document solution\n\n**If tests fail**:\n1. Review test output\n2. Identify failing test\n3. Fix code or test\n4. Re-run tests\n5. Document fix\n\n**If security issue found**:\n1. Identify vulnerability\n2. Update dependency\n3. Re-run audit\n4. Document fix\n\n---\n\n## Project Type Specific Guidance\n\n### Node.js/JavaScript Projects\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `package.json` - Dependencies and scripts\n- `tsconfig.json` - TypeScript config (if applicable)\n- `vite.config.js` or `webpack.config.js` - Build config\n- `.eslintrc` - Linting config\n- `.prettierrc` - Formatting config\n\n**Commands**:\n```bash\nnpm install\nnpm run build\nnpm run test\nnpm run lint\nnpm audit\n```\n\n### Python Projects\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `requirements.txt` - Dependencies\n- `setup.py` - Package setup\n- `pytest.ini` - Test config\n- `.pylintrc` - Linting config\n\n**Commands**:\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\npython -m pytest\npylint src/\nbandit -r src/\n```\n\n### Go Projects\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `go.mod` - Module definition\n- `go.sum` - Dependency checksums\n- `Makefile` - Build commands\n\n**Commands**:\n```bash\ngo mod download\ngo build\ngo test ./...\ngo vet ./...\n```\n\n### Java/Maven Projects\n\n**Key Files**:\n- `pom.xml` - Maven config\n- `src/main/java` - Source code\n- `src/test/java` - Tests\n\n**Commands**:\n```bash\nmvn clean install\nmvn test\nmvn package\n```\n\n---\n\n## Success Metrics\n\n### Completion Percentage Calculation\n\n```\nTotal Components: 100\nImplemented: 80\nTested: 75\nDocumented: 70\nDeployed: 0\n\nCompletion %: (80 + 75 + 70 + 0) / 400 = 56.25%\n\nOR\n\nCompletion %: (Implemented / Total) ร 100 = 80%\n```\n\n### Confidence Level\n\n```\nCode Coverage:      80% = 0.8\nTest Pass Rate:     100% = 1.0\nDocumentation:      90% = 0.9\nSecurity Audit:     100% = 1.0\nPerformance:        85% = 0.85\n\nConfidence = (0.8 + 1.0 + 0.9 + 1.0 + 0.85) / 5 = 0.91 = 91%\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting Guide\n\n### Common Issues\n\n**Issue**: Build fails with \"module not found\"\n```\nSolution:\n1. Delete node_modules\n2. Delete package-lock.json\n3. Run npm install\n4. Try build again\n```\n\n**Issue**: Tests fail with timeout\n```\nSolution:\n1. Increase test timeout\n2. Check for async issues\n3. Mock external calls\n4. Run tests individually\n```\n\n**Issue**: Security vulnerabilities found\n```\nSolution:\n1. Run npm audit fix\n2. Update vulnerable packages\n3. Re-run npm audit\n4. Document changes\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThis guide provides AI agents with:\n\nโ **Complete workflow** - 10 phases from start to finish\nโ **Decision trees** - Clear logic for every decision\nโ **Code templates** - Examples for every gap type\nโ **Commands** - Exact commands to run\nโ **Error handling** - How to handle failures\nโ **Success criteria** - Clear completion metrics\nโ **Project-specific guidance** - For different tech stacks\n\n**Result**: Any AI can execute this skill with 100% accuracy, regardless of project type, complexity, or initial state.\n

# Project Audit Skill - Operational Manual\n\n## Quick Reference\n\n### Entry Point\n```\nINPUT: Project (ZIP/Folder/Repository)\nโ\nExecute 10-Phase Workflow\nโ\nOUTPUT: Complete Project ZIP + Reports (100% Confidence)\n```\n\n### Phase Execution Matrix\n\n| Phase | Duration | Input | Output | Go/No-Go |\n|-------|----------|-------|--------|----------|\n| 1. Reception | 5 min | Raw project | Inventory | โ Always |\n| 2. Analysis | 15 min | Project files | Architecture | โ Always |\n| 3. Inventory | 10 min | Code files | Component list | โ Always |\n| 4. Testing | 20 min | Project | Build/test report | โ๏ธ May fail |\n| 5. Gap Analysis | 15 min | Findings | Gap list | โ Always |\n| 6. Gap Filling | 60+ min | Gap list | Implementations | โ If gaps exist |\n| 7. Code Writing | 30+ min | Specs | Production code | โ If gaps exist |\n| 8. QA | 20 min | Code | QA report | โ Always |\n| 9. Packaging | 10 min | Complete code | ZIP + docs | โ Always |\n| 10. Delivery | 5 min | Package | Final report | โ Always |\n\n---\n\n## Execution Commands\n\n### Phase 1: Reception\n```bash\n# Extract project\nunzip -q project.zip -d /workspace/project\ncd /workspace/project\n\n# Document initial state\necho \"=== PROJECT STRUCTURE ===\" > audit_log.txt\nfind . -type f | wc -l >> audit_log.txt\ndu -sh . >> audit_log.txt\nls -la >> audit_log.txt\n\n# Identify project type\necho \"=== PROJECT TYPE ===\" >> audit_log.txt\nls -la | grep -E \"package.json|requirements.txt|go.mod|pom.xml\" >> audit_log.txt\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Analysis\n```bash\n# Read critical files\necho \"=== README ===\" > analysis.txt\ncat README.md >> analysis.txt 2>/dev/null\n\necho \"\\n=== PACKAGE.JSON ===\" >> analysis.txt\ncat package.json >> analysis.txt 2>/dev/null\n\necho \"\\n=== ARCHITECTURE ===\" >> analysis.txt\nfind ./src -type f -name \"*.json\" | head -5 >> analysis.txt\n```\n\n### Phase 3: Inventory\n```bash\n# Count components\necho \"=== COMPONENT INVENTORY ===\" > inventory.txt\necho \"Frontend Components:\" >> inventory.txt\nfind ./src/components -type f | wc -l >> inventory.txt\n\necho \"Backend Services:\" >> inventory.txt\nfind ./src/api -type f 2>/dev/null | wc -l >> inventory.txt\n\necho \"Utilities:\" >> inventory.txt\nfind ./src/utils -type f 2>/dev/null | wc -l >> inventory.txt\n```\n\n### Phase 4: Testing\n```bash\n# Install and test\necho \"=== BUILD & TEST ===\" > test_report.txt\nnpm install 2>&1 | tail -20 >> test_report.txt\nnpm run build 2>&1 | tail -20 >> test_report.txt\nnpm run test 2>&1 | tail -20 >> test_report.txt\nnpm audit 2>&1 | head -30 >> test_report.txt\n```\n\n### Phase 5: Gap Analysis\n```bash\n# Analyze gaps\necho \"=== GAP ANALYSIS ===\" > gap_analysis.txt\necho \"Database Schema: $(test -f src/database/schema.sql && echo FOUND || echo MISSING)\" >> gap_analysis.txt\necho \"Authentication: $(grep -r \"auth\" src/ 2>/dev/null | wc -l) references\" >> gap_analysis.txt\necho \"Export Functions: $(grep -r \"export\" src/ 2>/dev/null | wc -l) references\" >> gap_analysis.txt\necho \"Tests: $(find . -name \"*.test.js\" -o -name \"*.spec.js\" 2>/dev/null | wc -l) test files\" >> gap_analysis.txt\n```\n\n### Phase 6-10: Implementation\n```bash\n# Create gap implementations\nmkdir -p src/database src/auth src/export\n\n# Implement database schema\ncat > src/database/schema.sql << 'EOF'\nCREATE TABLE users (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\nEOF\n\n# Implement authentication\ncat > src/auth/authPage.jsx << 'EOF'\nexport function AuthPage() {\n  // Implementation\n}\nEOF\n\n# Run QA\nnpm run lint\nnpm run test\nnpm run build\n\n# Package\nzip -r project-complete.zip . -x \"*/node_modules/*\" \"*/.git/*\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Decision Logic\n\n### Project Type Detection\n\n```javascript\nfunction detectProjectType(files) {\n  if (files.includes('package.json')) {\n    if (files.includes('tsconfig.json')) return 'TypeScript';\n    if (files.includes('vite.config.js')) return 'Vite';\n    if (files.includes('next.config.js')) return 'Next.js';\n    if (files.includes('expo.config.js')) return 'React Native';\n    return 'Node.js';\n  }\n  if (files.includes('requirements.txt')) return 'Python';\n  if (files.includes('go.mod')) return 'Go';\n  if (files.includes('pom.xml')) return 'Java';\n  if (files.includes('Dockerfile')) return 'Containerized';\n  return 'Unknown';\n}\n```\n\n### Gap Detection\n\n```javascript\nfunction detectGaps(projectFiles) {\n  const gaps = [];\n\n  // Check database\n  if (!projectFiles.includes('schema.sql')) {\n    gaps.push({ type: 'database', priority: 'critical' });\n  }\n\n  // Check authentication\n  if (!projectFiles.includes('AuthPage.jsx')) {\n    gaps.push({ type: 'auth', priority: 'critical' });\n  }\n\n  // Check exports\n  if (!projectFiles.includes('exportFunctions.js')) {\n    gaps.push({ type: 'export', priority: 'high' });\n  }\n\n  // Check tests\n  const testFiles = projectFiles.filter(f => f.includes('.test.'));\n  if (testFiles.length === 0) {\n    gaps.push({ type: 'testing', priority: 'high' });\n  }\n\n  return gaps.sort((a, b) => {\n    const priority = { critical: 0, high: 1, medium: 2, low: 3 };\n    return priority[a.priority] - priority[b.priority];\n  });\n}\n```\n\n### Completion Calculation\n\n```javascript\nfunction calculateCompletion(audit) {\n  const components = {\n    database: audit.hasDatabase ? 1 : 0,\n    auth: audit.hasAuth ? 1 : 0,\n    api: audit.hasAPI ? 1 : 0,\n    export: audit.hasExport ? 1 : 0,\n    tests: audit.hasTests ? 1 : 0,\n    docs: audit.hasDocs ? 1 : 0,\n    deployment: audit.hasDeployment ? 1 : 0\n  };\n\n  const total = Object.keys(components).length;\n  const completed = Object.values(components).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);\n\n  return {\n    percentage: (completed / total) * 100,\n    completed,\n    total,\n    components\n  };\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## File Templates\n\n### Database Schema Template\n```sql\n-- Users table\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,\n  name VARCHAR(255),\n  password_hash VARCHAR(255),\n  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Projects table\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (\n  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),\n  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),\n  name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,\n  description TEXT,\n  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Enable RLS\nALTER TABLE users ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\nALTER TABLE projects ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;\n\n-- RLS Policies\nCREATE POLICY \"Users can view own data\" ON users\n  FOR SELECT USING (auth.uid() = id);\n\nCREATE POLICY \"Users can view own projects\" ON projects\n  FOR SELECT USING (user_id = auth.uid());\n```\n\n### Authentication Component Template\n```jsx\nimport React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport { supabase } from '../api/supabaseClient';\n\nexport function AuthPage() {\n  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');\n  const [isLogin, setIsLogin] = useState(true);\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);\n  const [error, setError] = useState('');\n\n  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    setLoading(true);\n    setError('');\n\n    try {\n      if (isLogin) {\n        const { error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({\n          email,\n          password\n        });\n        if (error) throw error;\n      } else {\n        const { error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({\n          email,\n          password\n        });\n        if (error) throw error;\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      setError(err.message);\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"auth-container\">\n      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>\n        <input\n          type=\"email\"\n          value={email}\n          onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}\n          placeholder=\"Email\"\n          required\n        />\n        <input\n          type=\"password\"\n          value={password}\n          onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}\n          placeholder=\"Password\"\n          required\n        />\n        <button type=\"submit\" disabled={loading}>\n          {loading ? 'Loading...' : isLogin ? 'Login' : 'Sign Up'}\n        </button>\n      </form>\n      {error && <p className=\"error\">{error}</p>}\n      <button onClick={() => setIsLogin(!isLogin)}>\n        {isLogin ? 'Need an account?' : 'Have an account?'}\n      </button>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n```\n\n### Export Functions Template\n```javascript\nimport PDFDocument from 'pdfkit';\nimport { createWriteStream } from 'fs';\n\nexport async function exportToPDF(content, filename) {\n  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {\n    try {\n      const doc = new PDFDocument();\n      const stream = createWriteStream(filename);\n\n      doc.pipe(stream);\n      doc.fontSize(12).text(content);\n      doc.end();\n\n      stream.on('finish', resolve);\n      stream.on('error', reject);\n    } catch (error) {\n      reject(error);\n    }\n  });\n}\n\nexport async function exportToEPUB(content, filename) {\n  // EPUB export implementation\n}\n\nexport async function exportToDOCX(content, filename) {\n  // DOCX export implementation\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Validation Checklist\n\n### Pre-Execution\n- [ ] Project extracted successfully\n- [ ] Project type identified\n- [ ] Backup created\n- [ ] Workspace prepared\n\n### Post-Phase 4 (Testing)\n- [ ] Dependencies installed\n- [ ] Build successful\n- [ ] Tests passing (or documented)\n- [ ] No critical errors\n\n### Post-Phase 8 (QA)\n- [ ] Linting passed\n- [ ] Tests passing (>80% coverage)\n- [ ] Build successful\n- [ ] No security vulnerabilities\n- [ ] Documentation complete\n\n### Pre-Delivery\n- [ ] All gaps filled\n- [ ] All code tested\n- [ ] All documentation written\n- [ ] ZIP created and verified\n- [ ] Reports generated\n- [ ] Sign-off ready\n\n---\n\n## Performance Metrics\n\n### Time Estimates\n- Small project (< 50 files): 2-3 hours\n- Medium project (50-200 files): 4-6 hours\n- Large project (200+ files): 8-12 hours\n- Complex project with many gaps: 12-24 hours\n\n### Quality Metrics\n- Code coverage: >80%\n- Test pass rate: 100%\n- Linting errors: 0\n- Security vulnerabilities: 0\n- Documentation completeness: 100%\n\n---\n\n## Error Recovery\n\n### Build Fails\n```bash\n# Step 1: Check error\nnpm run build 2>&1 | grep -i \"error\"\n\n# Step 2: Clear cache\nrm -rf node_modules package-lock.json\n\n# Step 3: Reinstall\nnpm install\n\n# Step 4: Retry\nnpm run build\n```\n\n### Tests Fail\n```bash\n# Step 1: Review failures\nnpm run test 2>&1 | grep -i \"fail\"\n\n# Step 2: Fix issues\n# Edit failing test or code\n\n# Step 3: Retry\nnpm run test\n```\n\n### Security Issues\n```bash\n# Step 1: Audit\nnpm audit\n\n# Step 2: Fix\nnpm audit fix\n\n# Step 3: Verify\nnpm audit\n```\n\n---\n\n## Success Indicators\n\nโ **Phase 1**: Project extracted, type identified\nโ **Phase 2**: Architecture understood, files analyzed\nโ **Phase 3**: Components cataloged, count verified\nโ **Phase 4**: Build successful, tests passing\nโ **Phase 5**: Gaps identified, prioritized\nโ **Phase 6**: All gaps implemented\nโ **Phase 7**: Code written, tested, documented\nโ **Phase 8**: QA passed, no errors\nโ **Phase 9**: ZIP created, docs complete\nโ **Phase 10**: Delivery # Project Audit & Gap Analysis - Complete Workflow\n\n## Overview\n\nThis workflow provides a systematic approach to auditing any software project from initial reception to final delivery with 100% confidence and accuracy.\n\n## Phase 1: Project Reception & Initial Analysis\n\n### 1.1 Extract and Organize\n- Receive project (ZIP, folder, or repository)\n- Extract to working directory\n- Create backup copy\n- List all files and directories\n\n### 1.2 Identify Project Type\n- Check for `package.json` (Node.js)\n- Check for `requirements.txt` (Python)\n- Check for `go.mod` (Go)\n- Check for `pom.xml` (Java/Maven)\n- Check for `Dockerfile` (Containerized)\n- Determine primary tech stack\n\n### 1.3 Document Initial State\n- Total file count\n- Directory structure\n- Primary language/framework\n- Project size (lines of code)\n- Existing documentation\n\n## Phase 2: Deep Code Analysis\n\n### 2.1 File Inventory\n```bash\nfind . -type f -name \"*.js\" -o -name \"*.jsx\" -o -name \"*.ts\" -o -name \"*.tsx\" | wc -l\nfind . -type f | wc -l\n```\n\n### 2.2 Read Critical Files\n- `README.md` - Project overview\n- `package.json` - Dependencies and scripts\n- `app.config.ts` or similar - Configuration\n- `.env.example` - Environment variables\n- `Dockerfile` - Deployment info\n- Main entry point (`App.jsx`, `index.js`, etc.)\n\n### 2.3 Analyze Architecture\n- Frontend structure (if applicable)\n- Backend structure (if applicable)\n- API design and endpoints\n- Database schema (if applicable)\n- Authentication system\n- State management\n\n### 2.4 Code Quality Assessment\n- Linting configuration (ESLint, Pylint, etc.)\n- Formatting configuration (Prettier, Black, etc.)\n- Type checking (TypeScript, mypy, etc.)\n- Testing setup (Jest, Vitest, pytest, etc.)\n- CI/CD configuration\n\n## Phase 3: Component Inventory\n\n### 3.1 Frontend Components (if applicable)\n- Count total components\n- Identify custom components\n- Identify UI library usage (shadcn/ui, Material-UI, etc.)\n- Check component organization\n\n### 3.2 Backend Services (if applicable)\n- API endpoints\n- Database models\n- Authentication/Authorization\n- Business logic\n- Utilities and helpers\n\n### 3.3 Utilities and Libraries\n- NLP/ML modules\n- Processing functions\n- Helper utilities\n- API clients\n- Database clients\n\n## Phase 4: Testing & Validation\n\n### 4.1 Build Verification\n```bash\nnpm install\nnpm run build\n```\n\n### 4.2 Test Execution\n```bash\nnpm run test\nnpm run test:coverage\n```\n\n### 4.3 Dependency Check\n```bash\nnpm audit\nnpm outdated\n```\n\n### 4.4 Type Checking (if TypeScript)\n```bash\nnpm run type-check\n```\n\n## Phase 5: Gap Analysis\n\n### 5.1 Identify Missing Components\n- Database schema\n- Authentication UI\n- Export functions\n- API integrations\n- Deployment configuration\n- Documentation\n\n### 5.2 Assess Completeness\n- Frontend: ___% complete\n- Backend: ___% complete\n- Database: ___% complete\n- Tests: ___% complete\n- Documentation: ___% complete\n- Deployment: ___% complete\n\n### 5.3 Prioritize Gaps\n1. **Critical** - Blocks core functionality\n2. **High** - Affects major features\n3. **Medium** - Nice to have\n4. **Low** - Polish and optimization\n\n## Phase 6: Gap Filling\n\n### 6.1 Database Schema (if missing)\n- Design schema based on requirements\n- Create migration files\n- Add RLS policies\n- Create indexes\n- Write setup guide\n\n### 6.2 Authentication (if missing)\n- Create login/signup pages\n- Implement authentication logic\n- Add session management\n- Create Configure environment\n\n## Phase 7: Code Writing & Implementation\n\n### 7.1 Code Standards\n- Follow project conventions\n- Use consistent naming\n- Add proper error handling\n- Include input validation\n- Add logging\n\n### 7.2 Documentation\n- Add JSDoc/docstrings\n- Write inline comments\n- Create README sections\n- Add API documentation\n- Create setup guides\n\n### 7.3 Testing\n- Write unit tests\n- Write integration tests\n- Write E2E tests\n- Achieve >80% coverage\n- Test edge cases\n\n## Phase 8: Quality Assurance\n\n### 8.1 Code Review\n- Check for bugs\n- Verify logic correctness\n- Check performance\n- Verify security\n- Check accessibility\n\n### 8.2 Testing\n```bash\nnpm run test\nnpm run test:coverage\nnpm run lint\nnpm run type-check\n```\n\n### 8.3 Build Verification\n```bash\nnpm run build\nls -lh dist/\n```\n\n### 8.4 Documentation Review\n- Check README accuracy\n- Verify setup instructions\n- Check API documentation\n- Verify deployment console errors\n- [ ] No security issues\n- [ ] Performance acceptable\n- [ ] Accessibility compliant\n- [ ] Code quality high\n\n### 10.2 Delivery Package\n- Complete ZIP file\n- Completion report\n- Complete\n- Security audit: Passed\n- Performance: Acceptable\n\n## Key Principles\n\n1. **Thoroughness** - Leave no stone unturned\n2. **Accuracy** - Verify everything\n3. **Documentation** - name: project-audit-complete
description: Comprehensive project auditing and gap analysis from initial reception through final delivery. Use when analyzing any software project to identify what exists (100%), what's missing (100%), and how to complete it with 100% confidence and accuracy.
---

# Project Audit & Complete Gap Analysis

## Overview

This skill provides a systematic, thorough approach to auditing any software project from initial reception to final delivery with complete confidence and accuracy. It transforms a project from unknown state to fully documented, with all gaps identified and filled.

## When to Use This Skill

Use this skill when you need to:
- **Audit an existing project** - Understand what's there and what's missing
- **Complete an incomplete project** - Fill all gaps to 100% completion
- **Verify project quality** - Ensure all components meet standards
- **Prepare for production** - Get project deployment-ready
- **Document findings** - Create comprehensive audit reports
- **Deliver with confidence** - Guarantee 100% accuracy and completeness

## The Complete Workflow

The skill follows a 10-phase process:

### Phase 1: Project Reception & Initial Analysis
**Goal**: Understand the project structure and type

1. Extract project (ZIP, folder, or repository)
2. Identify project type (Node.js, Python, Go, etc.)
3. Document initial state (files, directories, size)
4. Create backup copy

**Deliverable**: Initial project inventory

### Phase 2: Deep Code Analysis
**Goal**: Understand the codebase completely

1. Read all critical files (README, package.json, config files)
2. Analyze architecture (frontend, backend, database)
3. Identify all components and modules
4. Map API endpoints and data flows

**Deliverable**: Architecture documentation

### Phase 3: Component Inventory
**Goal**: Catalog all existing components

1. Count frontend components
2. Identify backend services
3. List utilities and helpers
4. Document third-party integrations

**Deliverable**: Complete component list

### Phase 4: Testing & Validation
**Goal**: Verify everything works

1. Install dependencies
2. Run build process
3. Execute test suite
4. Check for errors and warnings

**Deliverable**: Build and test reports

### Phase 5: Gap Analysis
**Goal**: Identify what's missing

1. Compare against requirements
2. List missing components
3. Assess completeness percentage
4. Prioritize gaps (critical โ low)

**Deliverable**: Detailed gap analysis report

### Phase 6: Gap Filling
**Goal**: Implement all missing components

1. Database schema (if missing)
2. Authentication system (if missing)
3. API endpoints (if missing)
4. Export functions (if missing)
5. AI/ML features (if missing)
6. Deployment configuration (if missing)

**Deliverable**: Complete implementation

### Phase 7: Code Writing & Implementation
**Goal**: Write production-quality code

1. Follow project conventions
2. Add comprehensive error handling
3. Include input validation
4. Write JSDoc/docstrings
5. Create tests for new code

**Deliverable**: Production-ready code

### Phase 8: Quality Assurance
**Goal**: Ensure everything meets standards

1. Code review for bugs
2. Run full test suite
3. Check code quality (linting, formatting)
4. Verify documentation
5. Security audit

**Deliverable**: Quality assurance report

### Phase 9: Final Packaging
**Goal**: Create deliverable package

1. Create ZIP file with all code
2. Exclude node_modules, .git, etc.
3. Create completion report
4. Write setup and deployment guides

**Deliverable**: Complete project ZIP

### Phase 10: Final Delivery
**Goal**: Deliver with 100% confidence

1. Verify all tests passing
2. Confirm build successful
3. Check documentation complete
4. Validate against requirements
5. Sign off on completion

**Deliverable**: Project ready for production

## Key Principles

### 1. Thoroughness
- Examine every file
- Check every component
- Test every function
- Verify every requirement

### 2. Accuracy
- Double-check findings
- Verify test results
- Cross-reference documentation
- Validate against requirements

### 3. Documentation
- Document all findings
- Create comprehensive reports
- Write clear guides
- Provide examples

### 4. Testing
- Test all new code
- Run full test suite
- Check edge cases
- Verify integrations

### 5. Quality
- Follow best practices
- Maintain code standards
- Ensure security
- Optimize performance

## Bundled Resources

### Scripts

**`audit_project.py`** - Automated project analysis
```bash
python audit_project.py /path/to/project
```
Analyzes:
- File structure and statistics
- Critical files presence
- Dependencies
- Test coverage
- Code quality indicators

### References

**`audit_workflow.md`** - Detailed workflow guide
- 10-phase process breakdown
- Tools and commands
- Success criteria
- Key principles

**`gap_analysis_template.md`** - Gap analysis template
- Comprehensive checklist
- Scoring system
- Gap prioritization
- Recommendations

## Quick Start

### Step 1: Receive Project
```bash
# Extract the project
unzip project.zip
cd project
```

### Step 2: Run Initial Audit
```bash
# Use the audit script
python audit_project.py .
```

### Step 3: Deep Analysis
- Read README.md
- Check package.json
- Review architecture
- Examine components

### Step 4: Gap Analysis
- Use gap_analysis_template.md
- Document findings
- Prioritize gaps
- Create action plan

### Step 5: Fill Gaps
- Implement missing components
- Write tests
- Update documentation
- Verify quality

### Step 6: Final Delivery
- Run full test suite
- Create completion report
- Package project
- Deliver with confidence

## Confidence Metrics

Before final delivery, verify:

- โ **Code Coverage**: >80%
- โ **Test Pass Rate**: 100%
- โ **Build Status**: Successful
- โ **Linting**: No errors
- โ **Type Checking**: No errors
- โ **Documentation**: Complete
- โ **Security**: No vulnerabilities
- โ **Performance**: Acceptable

## Success Criteria

Project is complete when:

1. โ All files accounted for and analyzed
2. โ All components identified and documented
3. โ All gaps identified and prioritized
4. โ All gaps filled with production code
5. โ All code tested (>80% coverage)
6. โ All documentation complete
7. โ All quality checks passed
8. โ 100% confidence in delivery

## Common Gap Categories

### Database
- Schema design
- Table creation
- Migration scripts
- RLS policies
- Indexes

### Authentication
- Login/signup pages
- Session management
- Password recovery
- Permission system
- Token management

### API
- Endpoint implementation
- Request validation
- Error handling
- Rate limiting
- Documentation

### Export
- PDF generation
- EPUB creation
- DOCX export
- ZIP packaging
- Format validation

### AI/ML
- Model integration
- Agent implementation
- Processing functions
- Training data
- Validation

### Deployment
- Docker configuration
- Environment setup
- CI/CD pipeline
- Health checks
- Monitoring

## Tools & Commands Reference

### File Analysis
```bash
# Count files
find . -type f | wc -l

# Count lines of code
wc -l $(find . -name "*.js" -o -name "*.jsx")

# Directory size
du -sh .
```

### Dependency Analysis
```bash
# List dependencies
npm list

# Check for vulnerabilities
npm audit

# Check outdated packages
npm outdated
```

### Code Quality
```bash
# Run linter
npm run lint

# Format code
npm run format

# Type checking
npm run type-check
```

### Testing
```bash
# Run tests
npm run test

# Check coverage
npm run test:coverage

# Run E2E tests
npm run test:e2e
```

### Build
```bash
# Install dependencies
npm install

# Build project
npm run build

# Start development server
npm run dev
```

## Best Practices

1. **Be Thorough** - Don't skip steps
2. **Document Everything** - Write as you go
3. **Test Frequently** - Run tests after each change
4. **Follow Standards** - Use project conventions
5. **Communicate** - Keep stakeholders informed
6. **Verify Quality** - Double-check everything
7. **Get Feedback** - Review with team
8. **Iterate** - Improve based on feedback

## Next Steps

After using this skill:

1. Review the audit report
2. Prioritize gaps
3. Create implementation plan
4. Execute gap filling
5. Run quality assurance
6. Package and deliver
7. Gather feedback
8. Iterate if needed

## ๐ฏ ูุธุฑุฉ ุนุงูุฉ

Shadow Seven ุชููุฑ ูุฌููุนุฉ ุดุงููุฉ ูู APIs ููุนุงูุฌุฉ ุงููุตูุต ูุงูุชุตุฏูุฑ ูุงูุฐูุงุก ุงูุงุตุทูุงุนู.

### Base Configuration

```javascript
// vite.config.js
export default {
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': '/src',
      '@components': '/src/Components',
      '@pages': '/src/Pages',
      '@utils': '/src/utils',
      '@api': '/src/api',
      '@hooks': '/src/hooks'
    }
  }
```

---

## ๐ Authentication

### Supabase Client

**Location:** `src/api/supabaseClient.js`

```javascript
import { supabase } from '@/api/supabaseClient';

// Sign Up
const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({
  email: 'user@example.com',
  password: 'secure-password'
});

// Sign In
const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
  email: 'user@example.com',
  password: 'secure-password'
});

// Sign Out
const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();

// Get Current User
const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
```

### AuthContext

**Location:** `src/contexts/AuthContext.jsx`

```javascript
import { useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';

function MyComponent() {
  const { user, signIn, signOut, loading } = useAuth();
  
  if (loading) return <div>Loading...</div>;
  
  return (
    <div>
      {user ? (
        <button onClick={signOut}>Sign Out</button>
      ) : (
        <button onClick={() => signIn(email, password)}>Sign In</button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Methods:**
- `signIn(email, password)` - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฏุฎูู
- `signUp(email, password)` - ุฅูุดุงุก ุญุณุงุจ
- `signOut()` - ุชุณุฌูู ุงูุฎุฑูุฌ
- `user` - ุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุณุชุฎุฏู ุงูุญุงูู
- `loading` - ุญุงูุฉ ุงูุชุญููู

## ๐ง NLP APIs

### 1. Text Analyzer Enhanced

**Location:** `src/Components/upload/TextAnalyzerEnhanced.js`

#### analyzeAndCleanText()

ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ุดุงููุฉ ูููุตูุต ูุน ุชูููู 60-70% ูู ุงุณุชุฎุฏุงู LLM.

```javascript

const result = await analyzeAndCleanText(
  text,              // ุงููุต ุงูุฃุตูู
  language,          // 'ar' | 'en'
  callbacks          // Object with start, progress, complete
);
```

**Parameters:**

| Name | Type | Required | Description |
|------|------|----------|-------------|
| text | string | โ | ุงููุต ุงููุฑุงุฏ ูุนุงูุฌุชู |
| language | string | โ | ูุบุฉ ุงููุต ('ar' or 'en') |
| callbacks | object | โ | ุฏูุงู callback ููุชูุฏู |

**Callbacks Structure:**

```javascript
{
  start: (stageName) => void,      // ุนูุฏ ุจุฏุก ูุฑุญูุฉ
  progress: (stageName, data) => void,  // ุฃุซูุงุก ุงูุชูุฏู
  complete: (stageName) => void     // ุนูุฏ ุงูุชูุงู ูุฑุญูุฉ
}
```

**Return Value:**

```javascript
{
  cleaned_text: string,           // ุงููุต ุงูููุธู
  statistics: {
    original_words: number,       // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช ุงูุฃุตูู
    final_words: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช ุงูููุงุฆู
    original_chars: number,       // ุนุฏุฏ ุงูุฃุญุฑู ุงูุฃุตูู
    final_chars: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงูุฃุญุฑู ุงูููุงุฆู
    removed_pages: number,        // ุงูุตูุญุงุช ุงููุญุฐููุฉ
    removed_toc: boolean,         // ูู ุชู ุญุฐู ุงูููุฑุณุ
    removed_duplicates: number,   // ุงูุชูุฑุงุฑุงุช ุงููุญุฐููุฉ
    chapters_detected: number,    // ุงููุตูู ุงูููุชุดูุฉ
    processing_time: number       // ููุช ุงููุนุงูุฌุฉ (ms)
  },
  chapters: [
    {
      title: string,              // ุนููุงู ุงููุตู
      content: string,            // ูุญุชูู ุงููุตู
      wordCount: number,          // ุนุฏุฏ ุงููููุงุช
      number: number              // ุฑูู ุงููุตู
    }
  ],
  quality: {
    score: number,                // 0-100
    issues: string[],             // ุงููุดุงูู ุงูููุชุดูุฉ
    suggestions: string[]         // ุงูุชุฑุงุญุงุช ุงูุชุญุณูู
  },
  metadata: {
    language: string,
    processed_at: string,
    version: string
  }
}
```

**Example:**

```javascript

  start: (stage) => console.log(`๐ ุจุฏุฃ: ${stage}`),
  progress: (stage, data) => {
    console.log(`โณ ${stage}: ${data.progress}%`);
  },
  complete: (stage) => console.log(`โ ุงูุชูู: ${stage}`)
};

console.log('๐ ุงูุฅุญุตุงุฆูุงุช:', result.statistics);
console.log('๐ ุงููุตูู:', result.chapters.length);
console.log('โจ ุงูุฌูุฏุฉ:', result.quality.score);
```

### 3. ChunkProcessor

ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูุตูุต ูุจูุฑุฉ (ุญุชู 200k ูููุฉ) ุจุทุฑููุฉ ูุชูุงุฒูุฉ.

```javascript
  chunkSize: 10000,        // ูููุงุช ููู chunk

  maxConcurrent: 3         // ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูุชูุงุฒูุฉ

  largeText,

    // ูุนุงูุฌุฉ ูู chunk
```

### 4. CacheManager

**Location:** `src/lib/cache/CacheManager.js`

ูุธุงู ุชุฎุฒูู ูุคูุช ุซูุงุฆู (Memory + IndexedDB).

```javascript

  namespace: 'nlp',
  ttl: 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000  // 24 hours
});

// Get

// Delete

// Clear all
await cache.clear();
```

**Features:**
- โ Memory cache (ุณุฑูุน)
- โ IndexedDB cache (ุฏุงุฆู)

- โ Compression

```javascript
  const {
    manuscripts,
    loading,
    error,
    addManuscript,
    updateManuscript,
    deleteManuscript,
    refreshManuscripts
  } = useManuscripts();

  // Use manuscripts data
}
```

```javascript
import { useDebounce } from '@/hooks/useDebounce';

function SearchComponent() {
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const debouncedSearch = useDebounce(search, 500);

  useEffect(() => {
    // ุณูุชู ุงุณุชุฏุนุงุคู ุจุนุฏ 500ms ูู ุขุฎุฑ ุชุบููุฑ

}
```

## โ๏ธ Error Handling

### Error Types

```javascript
// NLP Errors
class NLPError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'NLPError';
    this.code = code;
  }
}

// Export Errors
class ExportError extends Error {
  constructor(message, format) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'ExportError';
    this.format = format;
  }
}

// API Errors
class APIError extends Error {
  constructor(message, status) {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'APIError';
    this.status = status;
  }
}
```

---

### Error Handling Best Practices

```javascript
try {
  const result = await analyzeAndCleanText(text, 'ar', callbacks);
} catch (error) {
  if (error instanceof NLPError) {
    console.error('NLP Error:', error.code, error.message);
    // Handle NLP-specific error
  } else if (error instanceof ExportError) {
    console.error('Export Error:', error.format, error.message);
    // Handle export-specific error
  } else {
    console.error('Unknown Error:', error);
    // Handle unknown error
  }
}
```

---

### ErrorBoundary Component

```javascript
import ErrorBoundary from '@/Components/ErrorBoundary';

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <YourComponent />
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}
```

```javascript
    showToast('ุชุญุฐูุฑ!', 'warning');
  };

  const handleInfo = () => {
    showToast('ูุนูููุฉ', 'info');
  };
```

# โ๏ธ Cloudflare Configuration Guide for Shadow Seven

This guide provides detailed instructions for configuring Cloudflare for your Shadow Seven deployment.

---

## ๐ Table of Contents

1. [Prerequisites](#prerequisites)
2. [DNS Configuration](#dns-configuration)
3. [SSL/TLS Configuration](#ssltls-configuration)
4. [Security Settings](#security-settings)
5. [Performance Optimization](#performance-optimization)
6. [Page Rules (Optional)](#page-rules-optional)
7. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)

---

## Prerequisites

Before you begin:

- โ Cloudflare account created
- โ Domain added to Cloudflare
- โ Nameservers updated to Cloudflare's nameservers
- โ Application deployed to server (45.224.225.96)
- โ Server is accessible via HTTP

---

## ๐ DNS Configuration

### Step 1: Access DNS Settings

1. Log in to [Cloudflare Dashboard](https://dash.cloudflare.com)
2. Select your domain from the list
3. Click on **DNS** in the left sidebar
4. Click **Add record** button

### Step 2: Add A Record for Subdomain

Configure the following:

| Setting | Value | Notes |
|---------|-------|-------|
| **Type** | `A` | IPv4 address |
| **Name** | `app` | Or your chosen subdomain (e.g., `shadow`, `platform`, `demo`) |
| **IPv4 address** | `45.224.225.96` | Your server IP |
| **Proxy status** | `Proxied` ๐ | Orange cloud icon - **IMPORTANT** |
| **TTL** | `Auto` | Automatic TTL |

**Example configurations:**

```
# Main subdomain
Type: A
Name: app
IPv4: 45.224.225.96
Proxy: Proxied (๐)
โ Results in: https://app.yourdomain.com

# Alternative subdomain names
Type: A
Name: shadow
IPv4: 45.224.225.96
Proxy: Proxied (๐)
โ Results in: https://shadow.yourdomain.com

# Root domain (if desired)
Type: A
Name: @
IPv4: 45.224.225.96
Proxy: Proxied (๐)
โ Results in: https://yourdomain.com
```

### Step 3: Add AAAA Record (IPv6) - Optional

If your server supports IPv6:

| Setting | Value |
|---------|-------|
| **Type** | `AAAA` |
| **Name** | `app` |
| **IPv6 address** | `Your IPv6 address` |
| **Proxy status** | `Proxied` ๐ |

### Step 4: Verify DNS Propagation

```bash
# Check DNS from your local machine
nslookup app.yourdomain.com

# Or use dig
dig app.yourdomain.com

# Online tools
# Visit: https://dnschecker.org
# Enter: app.yourdomain.com
```

**Expected Result:**
- Should resolve to Cloudflare's IP addresses (when proxied)
- Propagation takes 1-5 minutes typically

---

## ๐ SSL/TLS Configuration

### Step 1: Choose Encryption Mode

1. Go to **SSL/TLS** โ **Overview**
2. Choose the appropriate mode:

| Mode | Description | Recommended For |
|------|-------------|-----------------|
| **Off** | โ Not recommended | Never use |
| **Flexible** | Cloudflare โ๏ธ Browser: HTTPS<br>Cloudflare โ๏ธ Server: HTTP | Quick setup (temporary) |
| **Full** | Cloudflare โ๏ธ Browser: HTTPS<br>Cloudflare โ๏ธ Server: HTTPS (self-signed OK) | โ **Recommended** - After SSL cert installed |
| **Full (Strict)** | Cloudflare โ๏ธ Browser: HTTPS<br>Cloudflare โ๏ธ Server: HTTPS (valid cert required) | Best security (after Let's Encrypt) |

**Recommended Setup Process:**

```
1. Initially: Set to "Flexible"
   โ App accessible via HTTPS immediately
   
2. Install Let's Encrypt on server:
   ssh root@45.224.225.96
   certbot --nginx -d app.yourdomain.com
   
3. Change to "Full (Strict)"
   โ Maximum security achieved
```

### Step 2: Enable Always Use HTTPS

1. Go to **SSL/TLS** โ **Edge Certificates**
2. Enable **Always Use HTTPS**
3. This redirects all HTTP requests to HTTPS

### Step 3: Configure Minimum TLS Version

1. Under **Edge Certificates**
2. Set **Minimum TLS Version** to `TLS 1.2` or higher
3. Click **Save**

### Step 4: Enable Automatic HTTPS Rewrites

1. Under **Edge Certificates**
2. Enable **Automatic HTTPS Rewrites**
3. This fixes mixed content issues

### Step 5: Enable HTTP Strict Transport Security (HSTS)

โ๏ธ **Warning:** Only enable after testing HTTPS works properly!

1. Scroll to **HTTP Strict Transport Security (HSTS)**
2. Click **Enable HSTS**
3. Recommended settings:
   - Max Age: 6 months (15768000 seconds)
   - Include subdomains: Yes (if all subdomains use HTTPS)
   - Preload: No (initially)
   - No-Sniff Header: Yes

---

## ๐ก๏ธ Security Settings

### Step 1: Security Level

1. Go to **Security** โ **Settings**
2. Set **Security Level** to:
   - `High` - For maximum protection
   - `Medium` - Balanced (recommended)
   - `Essentially Off` - Minimal protection

**Recommended:** `Medium`

### Step 2: Bot Fight Mode

1. Enable **Bot Fight Mode**
2. This blocks known malicious bots

### Step 3: Browser Integrity Check

1. Enable **Browser Integrity Check**
2. Blocks browsers with bad reputations

### Step 4: Firewall Rules (Optional)

Create custom rules for additional protection:

1. Go to **Security** โ **WAF** โ **Firewall rules**
2. Click **Create firewall rule**

**Example Rule - Block countries:**
```
Rule Name: Block suspicious countries
Expression: (ip.geoip.country in {"XX" "YY"})
Action: Block
```

**Example Rule - Rate limiting:**
```
Rule Name: Rate limit API
Expression: (http.request.uri.path contains "/api/")
Action: Challenge
```

### Step 5: Enable Cloudflare WAF

1. Go to **Security** โ **WAF**
2. Enable **Cloudflare Managed Ruleset**
3. Enable **OWASP Core Ruleset** (if available in your plan)

---

## โก Performance Optimization

### Step 1: Auto Minify

1. Go to **Speed** โ **Optimization**
2. Enable **Auto Minify** for:
   - โ JavaScript
   - โ CSS
   - โ HTML

### Step 2: Brotli Compression

1. Under **Optimization**
2. Enable **Brotli** compression

### Step 3: Early Hints

1. Enable **Early Hints** (if available)
2. Speeds up page loads

### Step 4: Rocket Loader (Use with caution)

โ๏ธ **Warning:** May break React apps!

- **Recommended:** Leave **disabled** for React/SPA applications
- Enable only if tested and working

### Step 5: Caching Configuration

1. Go to **Caching** โ **Configuration**
2. Set **Caching Level** to `Standard`
3. Set **Browser Cache TTL** to `4 hours` or `1 day`

### Step 6: Enable Always Online

1. Under **Caching**
2. Enable **Always Online**
3. Serves cached version if server is down

### Step 7: Development Mode (for testing)

When making changes and need to bypass cache:

1. Go to **Caching** โ **Configuration**
2. Enable **Development Mode** (active for 3 hours)
3. Don't forget to disable after testing!

---

## ๐ Page Rules (Optional)

Page Rules allow fine-grained control. Examples:

### Rule 1: Cache Static Assets Aggressively

1. Go to **Rules** โ **Page Rules**
2. Click **Create Page Rule**

```
URL: app.yourdomain.com/assets/*
Settings:
  - Cache Level: Cache Everything
  - Edge Cache TTL: 1 month
  - Browser Cache TTL: 1 month
```

### Rule 2: Bypass Cache for API

```
URL: app.yourdomain.com/api/*
Settings:
  - Cache Level: Bypass
```

### Rule 3: Force HTTPS

```
URL: http://app.yourdomain.com/*
Settings:
  - Always Use HTTPS: On
```

**Free Plan:** 3 page rules
**Pro Plan:** 20 page rules

---

## ๐ Verify Configuration

### Test SSL/TLS

1. Visit: https://www.ssllabs.com/ssltest/
2. Enter: `app.yourdomain.com`
3. Target grade: A or A+

### Test Security Headers

1. Visit: https://securityheaders.com
2. Enter: `app.yourdomain.com`
3. Check for security issues

### Test Performance

1. Visit: https://www.webpagetest.org
2. Enter: `app.yourdomain.com`
3. Check load times and optimization

### Verify DNSSEC (Recommended)

1. Go to **DNS** โ **Settings**
2. Enable **DNSSEC**
3. Adds cryptographic signatures to DNS records

---

## ๐ Troubleshooting

### Issue: "Error 521 - Web server is down"

**Causes:**
- Application not running on server
- Nginx not running
- Server firewall blocking port 80/443

**Solutions:**
```bash
ssh root@45.224.225.96

# Check application
pm2 status
pm2 restart shadow-seven

# Check Nginx
systemctl status nginx
systemctl restart nginx

# Check firewall
ufw status
ufw allow 80/tcp
ufw allow 443/tcp
```

### Issue: "Error 522 - Connection timed out"

**Causes:**
- Server is down
- Firewall blocking Cloudflare IPs
- Application taking too long to respond

**Solutions:**
```bash
# Check server connectivity
ping 45.224.225.96

# Allow Cloudflare IPs
# Get IPs from: https://www.cloudflare.com/ips/
```

### Issue: "Error 525 - SSL handshake failed"

**Causes:**
- SSL/TLS mode set to "Full (Strict)" but no valid certificate on server
- Certificate expired
- Certificate mismatch

**Solutions:**
```bash
# Install/renew certificate
ssh root@45.224.225.96
certbot --nginx -d app.yourdomain.com

# Or change Cloudflare SSL mode to "Full" (not Strict)
```

### Issue: "Too many redirects"

**Causes:**
- SSL/TLS mode conflict
- Nginx redirecting HTTPS to HTTPS

**Solutions:**
1. Set Cloudflare SSL/TLS to "Full" or "Flexible"
2. Check Nginx configuration for redirect loops

### Issue: Mixed Content Warnings

**Causes:**
- Loading HTTP resources on HTTPS page

**Solutions:**
1. Enable **Automatic HTTPS Rewrites** in Cloudflare
2. Update code to use HTTPS or protocol-relative URLs

### Issue: Site not loading/502 Bad Gateway

**Solutions:**
```bash
# Check all services
ssh root@45.224.225.96 'pm2 status && systemctl status nginx'

# Check logs
ssh root@45.224.225.96 'pm2 logs shadow-seven --lines 50'
tail -f /var/log/nginx/error.log

# Restart everything
pm2 restart shadow-seven
systemctl restart nginx
```

---

## ๐ Monitoring & Analytics

### Cloudflare Analytics

1. Go to **Analytics & Logs** โ **Traffic**
2. View:
   - Requests over time
   - Bandwidth usage
   - Threats blocked
   - Response codes

### Setup Notifications

1. Go to **Notifications**
2. Add notification for:
   - SSL/TLS certificate expiration
   - Rate limiting threshold
   - DDoS attack detection

---

## โ Configuration Checklist

After setup, verify:

- [ ] DNS A record created for subdomain
- [ ] Proxy status is "Proxied" (orange cloud)
- [ ] SSL/TLS mode is "Full" or "Full (Strict)"
- [ ] Always Use HTTPS enabled
- [ ] Minimum TLS 1.2 or higher
- [ ] Auto Minify enabled
- [ ] Brotli compression enabled
- [ ] Security level set appropriately
- [ ] Bot Fight Mode enabled
- [ ] Browser Integrity Check enabled
- [ ] Site accessible via HTTPS
- [ ] SSL Labs test shows A or A+
- [ ] No mixed content warnings
- [ ] Caching working properly

---

## ๐ Best Practices

1. **Always use Proxy (orange cloud)**
   - Benefits: DDoS protection, caching, security
   - Your server IP is hidden

2. **Enable all security features**
   - WAF, Bot Fight Mode, Browser Integrity Check
   - Use firewall rules for additional protection

3. **Optimize caching**
   - Cache static assets aggressively
   - Use page rules for fine control

4. **Monitor your site**
   - Check analytics regularly
   - Set up notifications for issues

5. **Regular testing**
   - Test after any configuration changes
   - Use development mode during testing

6. **Keep certificates updated**
   - Let's Encrypt renews automatically
   - Monitor expiration dates

---

## ๐ Additional Resources

- [Cloudflare Learning Center](https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/)
- [Cloudflare Community](https://community.cloudflare.com/)
- [Cloudflare API Docs](https://developers.cloudflare.com/api/)
- [Cloudflare Status](https://www.cloudflarestatus.com/)

---

## ๐ Support

If you need help:

1. Check [Cloudflare Community](https://community.cloudflare.com/)
2. Review [Cloudflare Docs](https://developers.cloudflare.com/)
3. Contact Cloudflare Support (paid plans)
4. Check GitHub Issues for this project
